    var currentWebProtocol = "https";



    var hasInput = false;

    function setQuestion(){

        if ($("#searchQuestion").val() == 'Buscar'){

            $("#searchQuestion").val('');

            hasInput = true;

        }

    }



    function questionBlur(){

        var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();

        if (question == '' || question == 'Buscar'){

            hasInput = false;

            $("#searchQuestion").val('Buscar');

        }else{

            //[FBATGU-1148] when searchQuestion has value, hasInput is ture

            hasInput = true;

        }

    }



    function typeAheadCallBack(){



    }



    function search(){

        var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();

        if((question == '') || (!hasInput) || question.length<2){

            alert('Ingresa la palabra, producto o c√≥digo de lo que quieres buscar.');

            return false;

        }else

            return true;

    }

        $(document).ready(function(){

            var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();

            if (question != '' && question != 'Buscar'){

                hasInput = true;

            }



            var maxTypeahead = $("#maxTypeahead").val();

            var group = $("#group").val();

            var count = maxTypeahead * group;



            var typeAheadInfo = {isSearch:"true",maxTypeahead:count};



            if($('#enable_typeahead')!=null && $('#enable_typeahead').val()){

                if(currentWebProtocol === "http"){

                    $("#searchQuestion").autocomplete("/falabella-co/cartridges/typeAhead/typeaheadResults.jsp",{extraParams:typeAheadInfo,selectFirst:false,clickCallBack:typeAheadCallBack});

                }

                else{

                    $("#searchQuestion").autocomplete("/falabella-co/myaccount/typeahead/typeaheadResults.jsp",{extraParams:typeAheadInfo,selectFirst:false,clickCallBack:typeAheadCallBack});

                }

            }

        });

	function setNovioId(flag){

		$("#novioId").val(flag);

	}

	function checkInputIsValid(){

		var isValid=true;

		var month=$("#selectMonth").val();

		var year=$("#selectYear").val();

		var validateCode=$("#validationCodeInput").val();

		var code=$("#codeInput").val();

		$('#errorMsg').html("");

		if(month!=""&&year==""||month==""&&year!=""){

			isValid=false;

			var errorMessage = "por favor, introduzca la fecha completa";

			$('#errorMsg').html(errorMessage);

			return isValid;

		}

		if(validateCode!=""&&code==""||validateCode==""&&code!=""){

			isValid=false;

			$('#errorMsg').html("por favor, introduzca el c√≥digo completo");

			return isValid;

		}

		var nameRegex=/^[a-zA-Z√°√©√≠√≥√∫√?√â√?√ì√ö√º√ú√±√ë0-9 ,\\-]*$/;

		var novioNameHome = $("#novioNameHome").val();

		if(!nameRegex.test(novioNameHome)){

			isValid = false;

			$("#errorMsg").html("El nombre es no v√°lido.");

		}

		return isValid;

	}

	function checkInputValue(obj){

		var nameRegex=/^[a-zA-Z√°√©√≠√≥√∫√?√â√?√ì√ö√º√ú√±√ë0-9 ,\\-]*$/;

		var flag=nameRegex.test(obj.value);

		if(!flag){

			$('#errorMsg').html("El nombre es no v√°lido.");

			canSaveFlag=false;

		}else{

			$('#errorMsg').html("");

			canSaveFlag=true;

		}

	}

	function validatext(entrada) { 

	     tecla = (document.all) ? entrada.keyCode : entrada.which; 

	     if (tecla==8) return true;  //Tecla de retroceso (para poder borrar)                

	     if (tecla==0) return true;  //Tecla de tabular (para poder saltar entr los campos del formularios)

	     var patron = /\d/;

	       

	     aux = String.fromCharCode(tecla); 

	     return patron.test(aux); 

	}

	function clearInputValues(){

			$("#novioName").val("");

			$("#selectMonth").val("");

			$("#selectYear").val("");

			$("#codeInput").val("");

			$("#validationCodeInput").val("");

	}

	function setInputValue(suffix){

		$("#novioName").val($("#novioName"+suffix).val());

		$("#novioId").val($("#noviaId"+suffix).prop("checked"));

		$("#selectMonth").val($("#selectMonth"+suffix).val());

		$("#selectYear").val($("#selectYear"+suffix).val());

		$("#codeInput").val($("#codeInput"+suffix).val());

		$("#validationCodeInput").val($("#validationCodeInput"+suffix).val());

	}

	function searchNovios(suffix,id,url){

		setInputValue(suffix);

		var valid=checkInputIsValid();

		if(!valid){

			clearInputValues();

			return ;

		}

		var httpOrHttps = "";

			if("https" == httpOrHttps){

			 	url="/falabella-co/myaccount/includes/weddingSearch.jsp";

			}else{

				url="/falabella-co/browse/includes/weddingSearch.jsp"

			}

		

		var loginOptions = {

				url:url,

		      type:"POST",

		      success:function (data) {

		      	   $("#errorMsg").html("");

			       var errorMsg = $(data).find("#message").html();

				   $("#errorMsg").html(errorMsg);

				   $("#noviaIdHome").prop("checked",true);

				   if(errorMsg==null || errorMsg==""){

			       		parent.$("#"+id).colorbox({open:true});

			       }else{

			    	   var omnitureMsg = {

	    	            	omnitureBreadcrumbs:"Listas de Novios",

	    	            	omnitureS_prop12:$.trim(errorMsg)

	    	           };

	    	           omnitureMessageSend(omnitureMsg);

			       }

		      }, 

		      error:function (XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {

		      }

	      }

	      $.ajaxSetup({contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8"});

	      $("#novioSearchId").ajaxSubmit(loginOptions);

	}

</script>

		function saveCurrency(){

			$("#currencyCode").val($("#selecciona-moneda").val());

			$("#saveCurrencyForm").ajaxSubmit({type:"POST",async: false,success:successSaveCurrency,url:"/falabella-co/myaccount/includes/currencySaveSuccess.jsp"}); 

		}

		function successSaveCurrency(data){

			var mensajeErrorCurrency = $.trim(data);

			if(mensajeErrorCurrency.length==0||mensajeErrorCurrency==""){

				window.location.reload();

			}else{

				$("#showCurrencyMessage").html(mensajeErrorCurrency);

				$("#showSuccess").html("");

			}

		}

				$("#selecciona-moneda > option[value='"+paramCurrencyCode+"']").prop('selected',true);

   <script type="text/javascript">



    function checkCookieByName(cookieName){

        var documentCookies = document.cookie.split("; ");

        for (var i = 0, l = documentCookies.length; i < l; i++) {

            var parts = documentCookies[i].split("=");

            if(cookieName == parts[0]){

                return true;

            }

        }

        return false;

    }



    function ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity() {

        $.ajax({

             async: false,

             type: "POST",

             url: context+"/includes/ajaxFirstNameAndCartQuantity.jsp",

             dataType:"json",

             success: function(data){

                 if(data !=null && data != ""){

                     var firstName = data.ajaxHeaderFirstName;

         firstName=$.trim(firstName);

         if(firstName !=null && firstName != ""){

                 $("#freshLogin").html("Bienvenido! <a href='/falabella-co/myaccount/homeZP.jsp' rel='nofollow'><span id='greeting' class='linkSubrayado'>"+decodeURI(firstName)+"</span></a> o <a onclick='javascript:logout();return false;' href='#' rel='nofollow'><span class='linkSubrayado'>Cerrar sesi\u00f3n</span></a>");

         }

                     var quantity = data.ajaxHeaderCartQuantity;

                     if(quantity > 0){

                     $("#headQuantity").html(quantity+"  productos");

                     }

                 }

             }

         });

    }



    $(function(){

        if(checkCookieByName("DYN_USER_ID")){// only for the logged-in users



    if (!(typeof useDynamicDataCookie == "undefined") && useDynamicDataCookie) {



        //Here need to make an ajax call always when the referer url is login or register page.

        var isRefererLoginPage = false;

        var referrerUrl =  document.referrer;

        isRefererLoginPage = referrerUrl == '' || referrerUrl.indexOf('loginForm.jsp') > -1 || referrerUrl.indexOf('register.jsp') > -1;

        if(isRefererLoginPage){

          ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity();

        }else{

        //fetch data from another cookie

        var documentCookies = document.cookie.split("; ");

        for (var i = 0, l = documentCookies.length; i < l; i++) {

            var parts = documentCookies[i].split("=");

            if ("DYNAMIC_DATA_COOKIE" == parts[0]) {

            var dynamicDataCookieValue = parts[1].split("*");

            var firstName = dynamicDataCookieValue[0];

            if (firstName != null && firstName != "") {

                firstName = $.trim(firstName);

                $("#freshLogin").html("Bienvenido! <a href='/falabella-co/myaccount/homeZP.jsp' rel='nofollow'><span id='greeting' class='linkSubrayado'>" + decodeURI(firstName) + "</span></a> o <a onclick='javascript:logout();return false;' href='#' rel='nofollow'><span class='linkSubrayado'>Cerrar sesi\u00f3n</span></a>");

                // $("#greeting").html(firstName);

            }

            var quantity = dynamicDataCookieValue[1];

            if (quantity > 0) {

                $("#headQuantity").html(quantity + "  productos");

            }

            break;

            }

        }

        }

    } else { //post to ATG , get the fresh data

            ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity();

           }

  }

  else if (checkCookieByName("loyaltyCookie")) { // SSN-1126 - for loyalty site users

            if (quantity > 0) {

          }

        }

      });

    }

  }

  else

//Condicional Global de Ejecucion

if ((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/$")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/index.jsp")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/category\/")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/search\/")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/product\/")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/cart\/cart.jsp")).test(url) ||

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/checkout\/submitOrderSuccess.jsp")).test(url)

	){

		local_criteo_array = [];

		local_criteo_array.push(

			{event: "setAccount", account: 13929},

			{event: "setSiteType", type: "d"}

		);

		if ((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/$")).test(url) || (new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/index.jsp")).test(url)){

			//Home

			local_criteo_array.push(

				{event: "viewHome"}

			);

		} else if ((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/category\/")).test(url) || (new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/search\/")).test(url)) {

			//Category or PLP

			items = [];

			$(".detalle > a:eq(0), .detalle > a:eq(1), .detalle > a:eq(2)").each(function(key, element){

				items.push(($(element).attr("href").split("/"))[3]);

			});

			local_criteo_array.push(

				{event: "viewList", item: items}

			);

		} else if ((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/product\/")).test(url)) {

			//PDP

			local_criteo_array.push(

				{event: "viewItem", item: productId}

			);

		} else if ((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/cart\/cart.jsp")).test(url)) {

			//Cart

			 $(".omsProductoBolsa").each(function(key, element){

                               items.push({

                                      id : ($(element).find(".detalle > a").attr("href").split("/"))[3],

                                      quantity: parseInt($.trim($(element).find("select").val()))

                               });

                       });

			local_criteo_array.push(

				{event: "viewBasket", item: items}

			);

		} else if((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/checkout\/submitOrderSuccess.jsp")).test(url)){

		

			lines = s.products.split(";");

			if (lines.length > 3){

				lines.splice(lines.length - 4, 1);

			}

			line_items = [];

			for(index = 0; index < lines.length; index = index + 3)

			{

				   item = {};

				   item.id = lines[index];

				   item.quantity = lines[index + 1];

				   item.price = Number(lines[index + 2].replace(",",""));

				   line_items.push(item);

			}

			local_criteo_array.push(

							deduplication: '1', item: line_items

/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element anchor element

 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain

 */

function isOutOfDomain(element) {

    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {

            return false;

        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {

            return true;

        }

        return true;

    }

    return false;

}

            isMenuLink = true;

        }

            return;

        finalCondition = isMenuLink;

        return finalCondition;

                if (rgx.indexOf(menuLink.textContent.trim()) > -1) {

                    var indexColumn = i;

                    var thisSlpTitle = ui.isSLP() ? /__title/.test(menuLink.className) : /_submenuTitle/.test(menuLink.className);

                    if (thisSlpTitle) {

                        if (menuLink.textContent === el.querySelector('[class*="_submenuTitle"]').textContent) {

                            switch (type) {

                                case "column":

                                    order = indexColumn;

                                    break;

                                case "row":

                                    order = /<\/a>/.test(menuLink.outerHTML) ? indexColumn = 0 : indexColumn + 1;

                                    break;

                                default:

                                    break;

                            }

                        }

                    } else {

                        var isSLPListElement = ui.isSLP() ? el.querySelectorAll('li') : el.querySelectorAll("[class*=ThirdLevelItems_listElements]");

                        // var thirdLink = windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                        var thirdLink = function() {

                            if (ui.isSLP()) {

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"] [class*="secondLevelMenu__content"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                            } else {

                                // return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuMobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel] li') : isSLPListElement;

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="activeMobileThirdLevel"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems]') : isSLPListElement;

                            }

                        };

                        thirdLink = [].slice.apply(thirdLink());

                        thirdLink.map(function(el, i) {

                            if (el.textContent.trim() === menuLink.textContent.trim()) {

                                switch (type) {

                                    case "column":

                                        order = indexColumn;

                                        break;

                                    case "row":

                                        order = ui.isSLP() ? i - 1 : i + 1;

                                        break;

                                    default:

                                        break;

                                }

                            }

                        });

                    }

                }

            }

        });

        return order;

    }

};



function execute() {



    var firstLevelDescription, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition,

        columnOrder, rowOrder, firstLevelCollection, linksCollection, columnCollection;



    var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

    var topLevelMenu = document.querySelector('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') ? document.querySelectorAll('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') : document.querySelectorAll('.fb-masthead__new-hamburger-menu [class*="_firstCategories"],[class*="CategoryMenuButton-module_menu-toggle-button"]');

    //var validateServer = digitalData.page.serverName;

    if (topLevelMenu.length === 0)

        return;

    document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {

        try {

            var menuLink = windowW ? event.target : event.target.closest('a');

            var anchorLink = menuLink ? menuLink.closest('a') || menuLink.querySelector('a') : null;



            if (menuLink && ui.approvedTrackClick(menuLink)) {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition() + 1;

                firstLevelDescription = ui.firstLevelDescription();

                var linkTo = event.target || event.target.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.querySelector('[class*="submenuTitleToggleActive"]');

                var theParent = function() {

                    if (windowW) {

                        return linkTo;

                    } else {

                        if (menuLink.className.indexOf("thirdLevelMenu--link") > -1 || menuLink.className.indexOf("ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLi") > -1) {

                            return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement

                        } else {

                            return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;

                        }

                    }

                };

                secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());

                thirdLevelDescription = menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "" && menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "arrow" ? menuLink.textContent.trim() : secondLevelDescription;



                columnOrder = ui.order(menuLink, 'column');

                rowOrder = ui.order(menuLink, 'row') === -1 ? 0 : ui.order(menuLink, 'row');



                if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                    localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                    //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                }



                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



            }

            if (/img_banner/.test(event.target.className)) {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition();

                var topCategory = event.target.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.closest('[class*="submenuStage"]').querySelector('[class*="FirstLevelItems_menuElementsHover"]').textContent;

                var ImgName = event.target.src.match(/([^\/]+)\?|([^\/]+)\.gif|([^\/]+)\.jpg|([^\/]+)\.jpeg/)[0].replace('?', '');

                if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                    localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                }

                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', topCategory + '|' + 'B1' + '|' + ImgName + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + '50' + '|' + '1');

            }

            if (event.target.closest('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_category-content-container"],[class*="CategoryMenuMobile-module_mobile-menu-container"]')) {

                if (window.screen.width < 1024) {

                    //dosomething

                    if (event.target.closest('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]') || event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category"]') && event.target.localName !== "svg" && !/CategoryMenuButton-module_hamburger/i.test(event.target.className)) {

                        columnCollection = [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[data-testid="first-level-category"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]'));

                        linksCollection = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]') ? [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="MenuBody-module_leaf-category-item"]')) : [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-2"]').parentElement.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[class*="MenuBody-module_leaf-category-item"]'));

                        firstLevelCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[class*="AccordionContent-module_level-button-1"]'));



                        firstLevelPosition = firstLevelCollection.indexOf(document.querySelector('[class*=AccordionContent-module_level-button-1][class*=AccordionContent-module_active]')) + 1;

                        firstLevelDescription = document.querySelector('[class*=AccordionContent-module_level-button-1][class*=AccordionContent-module_active]').innerText;

                        columnOrder = columnCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('[data-testid="first-level-category"]').querySelector('[class*=AccordionContent-module_level-button-2][class*=AccordionContent-module_active]'));

                        if (columnCollection[columnOrder] === undefined) {

                            return;

                        }



                        secondLevelDescription = columnCollection[columnOrder].innerText;

                        thirdLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category"]').innerText : columnCollection[columnOrder].innerText;

                        rowOrder = !event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]') ? 0 : linksCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category"]')) + 1;

                        if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                            localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                            //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                        }

                        localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



                    }

                } else {

                    if (event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') || ('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]')) {

                        columnCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[class*="SubCategories-module_tab-container"] ul'));

                        linksCollection = [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]'));

                        firstLevelCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid="desktop-menu-category-button"]'))



                        firstLevelPosition = firstLevelCollection.indexOf(document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"]')) + 1;

                        firstLevelDescription = document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"] span').innerText;

                        columnOrder = columnCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('ul'));

                        secondLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('ul').querySelector('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        thirdLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        rowOrder = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? 0 : linksCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]')) + 1;

                        if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                            localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                            //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                        }

                        localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



                    }



                }

            }

            if (menuLink && windowW && !ui.approvedTrackClick(menuLink) && (menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'))) {



                var listElement = menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]');

                var menuItems = Array.from(listElement.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'));

                var menuDescription = listElement.innerText.trim().replace(/\r?\n|\r/g, ' ');

                menuDescription = menuDescription.startsWith('Tienes') ? 'Mis CMR puntos' : menuDescription;



                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + 'H' + (menuItems.indexOf(listElement) + 1) + '|0|0');

            }



            if (_satellite && localStorage.getItem('topLevelMenuCoords') && isOutOfDomain(anchorLink)) {

                _satellite.track('OOD_CALL');

            }

        } catch (ex) {}

    });

}



execute();

});</script>
